The service is good. The boss, the proprietress, and the lady at the front desk are all very enthusiastic. They provide excellent services such as introducing the mountain route, tea ceremony, and borrowing trekking poles.
The food is good. I booked this place because I valued the food. It was really delicious haha. Breakfast and dinner are both unique and delicious, and the homemade tea and refreshments are also great, making them perfect as souvenirs.
The experience was great, and the B&B provided fireworks just in time for New Year's Day. Itâ€™s important to mention here that the owner of the B&B can take you to the top of the nearby Chashan Mountain to watch the sunrise and sunset. You donâ€™t have to bother going to the Huangshan Scenic Area. You can drive directly to the top of the mountain and you can see the super beautiful scenery that is not inferior to other mountain tops.

The hotel is a 5-minute drive from the scenic spot. The hotel will provide free shuttle service, so you will not feel inconvenienced. On the contrary, because the hotel is a certain distance away from the noisy tourist gathering place, you will feel the tranquility that Huangshan should have. Behind the hotel is a tea mountain, and you can drink the stream water from the mountain directly. It feels really great!

The store has its own tea mountain and tea factory. When they are not busy, they may take you to have tea and learn about the local culture. You can also buy their own tea (their black tea has won the title of local tea king) and related merchandise. All in all a very special experience.

I hope the friends in the store can continue to pass on the happiness. If you are lucky enough to come here: I hope you like it here, and please take care of the plants and trees here & be nice :)
